The Military and Political Affairs of the Puppet Organization in the Past Year: Military Departments Established in Name Only, Organization in Great Disorder; Using Propaganda to Anesthetize Soldiers 94

Changchun Correspondence. Recently, Zhang Daojinghui, Minister of Military and Political Affairs of the puppet organization, published "The Military and Political Affairs of Manchukuo," revealing the situation of the puppet organization's military and political affairs, which are entirely trained and compiled by the Japanese. The military officers are also Japanese, probably to prevent the puppet organization from defecting. The details are recorded as follows:

History of the Puppet Military and Political Affairs 95

Since the establishment of the puppet organization's Ministry of Military and Political Affairs in March of the first year of Datong, General Ma Zhanshan, due to the loss of the Hu-Hai Road and the temporary government of Hailun Province being under heavy military pressure, and because he was isolated and without assistance, had to temporarily respond to the Japanese threats. He also wanted to probe the truth of the Japanese army and the inner workings of the puppet organization, so he endured humiliation and temporarily assumed the position of Minister of the puppet Military and Political Affairs. After only two months, General Ma secretly revolted, leaving the puppet ministerial position to be concurrently held by Deputy Minister Wang Jingxiu. However, the real power of the military and political affairs was completely controlled by the Japanese, and the general puppets were no different from walking corpses. A puppet Central Training Office was also established, which only admitted the children of puppet officers. The director was concurrently held by Wang Jingxiu. The office was located in Liaoning and hired Japanese as instructors, using this to build the foundation of Japanese-puppet friendship. A puppet military training department was established, with Wang Zhiyau appointed as the colonel chairman, specializing in using propaganda materials such as texts and cartoons to lure and anesthetize our compatriots. It also published the "Military Weekly," which was distributed to various units of the puppet army to induce soldiers to absolutely obey the puppet organization, confirm Japan as a friendly country, and not to resist. In the name of unifying horse administration, the military animal husbandry farms of Heilongjiang Province were ordered to be directly under the jurisdiction of the puppet Ministry of Military and Political Affairs.

Establishment of Military Propaganda Department 96

From September of the first year of Datong to May of the second year, it was a period of military affairs, but the volunteer army continued to rise up, and the military period was extended. A puppet military propaganda department was established, publishing propaganda materials such as the "Military Weekly" and slogans, leaflets, cartoons, and military pamphlets, which were distributed to each puppet army unit, one copy per person. Airplanes were also used to fly to various places to distribute them, anesthetizing soldiers and the people, falsely singing the Wangdao Doctrine, and intending to make the puppet army recognize the Chinese as enemies and regard the Japanese as friendly countries. Every week, Japanese military officers gave lectures to the puppet army, which were translated by traitors, saying that the puppet army must be directly under the jurisdiction of the Japanese army. Everyone must never recognize themselves as a Chinese nation. All the pamphlets issued must be memorized. If anyone is illiterate, they must remember them firmly during the lecture. Otherwise, if they cannot answer when asked, they will be severely punished. In order to eliminate the power of our volunteer army, the Japanese also rewarded those who reported the family members of the volunteer army after they were discovered by the puppet army, and those who knew but did not report were guilty of treason. After the Yuguan Incident and the fall of Rehe, the Japanese and puppets considered the military affairs to have come to an end, so they changed the "Military Weekly" to the "Elite Military Weekly." Japanese language training classes were added to the army to assimilate our nation, so that the puppet army would lose its national concept, be loyal to the Japanese and puppets.

Japanese Undertake Military Surveying 97

The Japanese invasion of the Northeast in military affairs used all possible means. After the establishment of the puppet organization, the Japanese used the slogan of Japanese-puppet friendship to anesthetize the ignorant Northeast compatriots. Regarding important military matters, military surveying and military maps are based on the Japanese-puppet agreement. All military surveying of the puppet country is undertaken by the Japanese. In name, a surveying section is added to the staff department of the puppet Ministry of Military and Political Affairs to assist the entrusted agency in handling surveying administrative matters, but in reality, it is entirely controlled by the Japanese. Because military surveying is related to national defense secrets, it is feared that it will be spied on by foreigners. Therefore, regarding military surveying, after the puppet country's surveying department has measured the detailed map, it will be printed and forwarded to the puppet Ministry of Military and Political Affairs by the Japanese Army Surveying Department, and then forwarded to major bookstores for public sale by the surveying section within the puppet Ministry of Military and Political Affairs. The procedures are very cautious.

Japanese Youth Fill Military Officer Positions 98

After the establishment of the puppet organization under Japanese patronage, all the Northeast armies revolted one after another. In order to prevent the activities of the volunteer army, the Japanese recruited unemployed workers, peasants, and youths day and night for training to form a basic army. On the one hand, they could be loyal to the puppet country, and on the other hand, they could strike at the volunteer army and maintain local stability. However, the volunteer army's momentum was too great, and there was nothing to be done. Therefore, people were sent to buy them off, but this was not very effective. Seeing this, the Japanese military department forcibly selected 400 Japanese military academy students and sent them to the Northeast to organize and train the army, and strictly monitor the army to prevent any defection. These young military officers went to the Northeast in September of this year and were assigned to the puppet army to take charge of affairs. In reality, the Japanese military department is using this to prevent the army from defecting and can implement a kind of military invasion in advance. (Northeast News Agency)

Local Austerity Plan in Bandit Suppression Areas: He Jian Formulated Eight Items; Jiang Clarified and Ordered Compliance 99

Nanchang Correspondence. Chairman Jiang, in response to He Jian's presentation of eight austerity plans for local expenditures in counties within the western bandit suppression area, which were reviewed and approved yesterday, issued separate instructions for compliance and also instructed the provincial governments to inform them. The original presentation and instructions are as follows:

He Jian's presentation stated: "One, it is to present eight austerity plans for local expenditures in counties within the bandit suppression area under our jurisdiction, requesting review and approval. Our department has, for the finances of each county within the bandit suppression area, formulated seven key points for the reorganization of county local finances, which have been approved by Your Excellency based on the administrative implementation plan and the promulgated regulations for reorganizing county local finances, and promulgated to each county, with separate documents presented for review and approval on file. I believe that the usual administrative expenditures of each county within the bandit suppression area must first strive to tighten them up in order to provide relief and conform to the principles of reorganization. Therefore, I have established eight austerity plans for county local expenditures based on the provisions of the second section and second item regarding usual administration in the plan, clearly defining standards to avoid disputes. In addition to issuing orders to each county within the bandit suppression area to comply, and notifying each competent provincial government for review and transmission, I have compiled and presented the plans with this document to Your Excellency for review and approval, which would be very convenient."

Chairman Jiang's instructions stated: "One, all submitted documents are understood. After reviewing the eight austerity plans for county local expenditures, there are still areas that should be considered. Specific instructions are given below. (1) The first item of the plan should be changed to: 'In each county within the bandit suppression area, the local administrative organs are the county government, the county finance committee, and the county clearing and resettlement committee. However, if a finance bureau has already been established and is jointly managed by the county, without additional expenses, it should be retained. Otherwise, no other redundant organs are allowed.' (2) The fourth item of the plan should be changed to: 'For each county's financial matters, all matters relating to the collection and remittance of provincial taxes are handled by the county government or the county finance bureau. All matters relating to county local finances are handled by the county finance committee. With the exception of the county finance committee's expenses, all financial administrative expenses for county funds are discontinued.' (3) The seventh item should be changed to: 'Charitable undertakings, with the exception of established medical institutions which should be retained, vaccination and epidemic prevention matters which should continue to be carried out, and relief, appeasement, and accommodation during the clearing and suppression period which are most urgent, should all be merged into the county clearing and resettlement committee for concurrent management. Other matters that can be delayed should have their expenses discontinued.' (4) The second, third, fifth, sixth, and eighth items of the plan are all acceptable and are approved for implementation. The following four items, after being revised separately by the General Headquarters, should be resubmitted for record. There are also additional instructions for implementing the austerity measures: (1) The local areas of Gao'an, Anyi, Yongxiu, Qingjiang, Xiajiang, Ji'an, Wuning, Xiushui, Jing'an, and Pingxiang in Jiangxi Province are considered tranquil, and the public security expenses are available, and the management is relatively successful. The public security bureaus of each county should be exempted from merging according to the other provisions of item two of the plan. (2) In the future, for each county that merges public security bureaus, the police officers who are physically strong, have been trained, and have firearms can be temporarily incorporated into the defense team, but the number of people, expenses, firearms, and other items to be merged must be compiled and sent to the competent provincial government for the record. (3) The education expenses of Gao'an, Anyi, Qingjiang, Wuning, Pingxiang, Yichun, and Fengxin in Jiangxi, are more than 30,000 and less than 10,000 yuan. The schools are still developed, and the results are good. The education bureaus of each county should be exempted from merging according to the other provisions of item three of the plan. (4) The various expenses for judicial administration in each county, which were originally paid by the provincial treasury, are still paid by the county government or finance bureau under the provincial tax item. In addition to ordering the Jiangxi provincial government to be informed, they should immediately investigate and handle. "(October 24, Datong News Agency)

Inspection Notes of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan and Hubei by Special Correspondent Ren An of this Newspaper 100

Impressions of Changsha 101

Changsha Correspondence. It is very convenient to travel from Xiangtan to Changsha, with ships on the water and cars on land. The reporter took the 4:00 AM boat and arrived in Changsha around 9:00 AM. According to Jin Zhuangchun, the section chief of the secretarial department of the provincial government, the general situation of Hunan Province's construction and the strategy of suppression is roughly: "Our Hunan has been troubled for many years. In 1911, it suffered a red disaster. Before it had time to recuperate, an unprecedented flood in the following year flooded the entire territory. The bandits in the border area also took the opportunity to stir up trouble. Last year, the financial situation became even more depleted due to the abundant disaster, and both cities and rural areas suffered the consequences. Fortunately, it has now managed to overcome the difficulties and is gradually reaching a better state. As for the strategy of suppression, military and political affairs have always been used together. Military force can only suppress tangible bandits, while politics can clear intangible bandits. Specifically, in addition to trying our best to publicize the Three People's Principles and severely refute communism, we are also strictly conducting census, handling joint security, and paying special attention to neighboring bandit areas and recovered bandit areas. Considering its effect, when forming joint security, suspicious people will not be able to join. After joint security is formed, they will supervise each other, so that bandits have nowhere to hide. They advise each other not to work in Hunan, so it is generally recognized that this is an important matter for suppression, and it is still being worked hard. As for construction matters, such as highways, agriculture and forestry, mining, industry, commerce, and water conservancy, each has a dedicated agency to implement according to plan."

Changsha is the capital of Hunan Province, with many agencies and a dense population. It is also known for its convenient water and land transportation, and industry and commerce have always been developed. However, according to Han Zigang, a friend who has been doing business in Changsha for a long time, "The business of various industries in Changsha City was very prosperous in the past. After the devastation of Lord Yang and the trouble of the red atmosphere, the countryside has been collapsing day by day, and the villagers have been flocking to the cities. Although the population has increased, the purchasing power has decreased, and business failures due to frequent taxes and difficult capital turnover are heard every day. " I then visited Taixin Park. On the way, on the doors of the people's houses, I often saw the words "Residence of officials, no disturbances allowed" written by Commander-in-Chief He. The government is deliberately protecting the residence of civil servants, but it seems that there is no such thoroughness for civilian residences. I then entered the park, climbed up to Tiangong Pavilion, which is as high as the factory chimney. Looking down on the whole city, there is a panoramic view. The pavilion hangs many plaques and couplets of celebrities, and there are children's sports grounds and zoos, etc., but the scale is very small. The forests and lawns, as well as the parks, are not very large. Leaving the park and heading south for about a mile, there is Baisha Well, a famous well in Changsha. The spring water protrudes from the ground, shaped like Baotu Spring in Jinan. Watermen take it in turn, and it is endless day and night, because each load of river water costs only a few copper coins, while this can be sold for a dollar or two. Crossing the Xiangjiang River and heading west for about seven or eight miles is Mount Yuelu, the first scenic spot in Changsha. The houses at the foot of the mountain are arranged like stars. It is the former Yuelu Academy and the current Hunan University. On the mountainside are the tombs of Cai Songpo, Huang Xing, and others. In the lush forest and bamboo, there are many ancient temples and monasteries, which are worth visiting. The temple on the top of the mountain, named Yunlu Palace, rises above the clouds. Climbing up, you can see the colors of the mountains evenly divided, and the Xiangjiang River surrounds it. It is truly a scenic spot. At that time, there were five or six Japanese people carrying cameras and telescopes, taking pictures of all the scenic spots and arbitrarily looking at the high and distant places with mirrors, recording them one by one. These people once surrounded and read an ancient plaque, and did not leave for a long time. The reporter wanted to take a picture and asked them not to block the object, but they simply ignored it. It is regrettable that the guest is acting as the host.

Monk from Zhizhi Nunnery in Songjiang Caught in Adultery 102

Xu Yapin, a resident outside the West Gate of this county, has been working as a partner in Shenchang Rice Shop. He married Zhang, who is now twenty-two years old. They have been married for almost six years, but she is naturally frivolous and fond of embellishment. Xu has repeatedly advised her to change her ways, but to no avail. Recently, she had an affair with a monk named Changrong from Zhizhi Nunnery. The monk, on the twenty-fourth, took advantage of Xu's absence to collect debts and went to Zhang's residence to spend the night. Unexpectedly, Xu returned home around eleven o'clock that evening and knocked on the door. Zhang opened the door, and Xu noticed her flustered appearance. He then searched the house and dragged Changrong out from under the bed. He then took both Changrong and Zhang to the Third Public Security Precinct to report the incident. After preliminary interrogation by Inspector Qu, the case was deemed to involve adultery and was transferred to the County Court Procuratorate for investigation yesterday. The plaintiff was ordered to return home, and the two defendants were detained pending review.

Thorough Investigation Ordered in Suzhou of Charges Against Changshu County Magistrate 103

Changshu County Magistrate Zhou Yiheng has been accused by citizens of the county, including Hu Du and Qian Huasheng, in a petition to the Department of Civil Affairs. They accuse Zhou of corruption, abuse of power, opium addiction, and employing cronies, and request his dismissal and investigation. Upon receiving the petition, the Department of Civil Affairs instructed the Commissioner's Office of the Third Administrative Inspectorate to conduct a thorough investigation to serve as a basis for review.

Hearing on Labor Dispute at Railway Hotel 104

The labor dispute at the Dingjia Lane Railway Hotel once led to a city-wide strike. The standoff between labor and management has lasted for months without resolution. Now, the County Party Headquarters here received an instruction yesterday (the 26th) from the Provincial Party Headquarters, which in turn received an instruction from the Central People's Movement Committee, to work with various agencies and the hospitality industry union to find employment for unemployed workers such as Zhu Haitang and Jin Quan.

Women's Association Cracks Down on Private Prostitution 105

The Wuxian Women's Association, recognizing the large number of private prostitutes in Suzhou, believes that they should be cracked down on. The board of directors has decided to establish a reformatory for prostitutes, conduct a survey of the prostitute population in order to persuade them to reform, and also send a letter to the Minsheng Singer and Dancer Association, urging them to register with the association as soon as possible. However, the financial problem is extremely difficult, and they are currently looking for solutions.

Wuxi Defense Corps Holds Examination 106

The County Defense Committee of this county, in order to thoroughly reorganize the county's defense corps, has re-investigated the household registration, provided training, and formulated a training program. Starting from November 1st, a special training class will be organized, requiring district chiefs to send corps members to the county before the 25th of this month. The examination will be held on the 16th. The location of the special training class is the former site of the Labor Hospital in Ba'er Lane. Yesterday was the examination date. One hundred and sixty-three corps members reported for the examination. At 8 a.m., the examination was held at the police training school of the Public Security Bureau. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu and Directors Zhu and Xu were present to supervise the examination. The examination subjects included Chinese language, Party ideology, arithmetic, practical military skills, and command (platoon training). In the afternoon at one o'clock, the physical fitness of the corps members was also examined. Currently, sixty students have been admitted. However, because the number of applicants was insufficient, a supplementary examination will be scheduled and classes will be held again.

Police Officer in Disguise Captures Bandit, Solves Case 107

Qu Haitao, an employee of Deda Coal Oil Company near Tonghui Bridge in this county, went to Huishan with two friends around one o'clock in the afternoon the day before yesterday. They returned to the city around seven o'clock that evening. While passing the intersection of Wulijie and Shanlukou, they were suddenly accosted by four thugs who brandished pistols and blocked their way. They were stripped of three long robes, robbed of sixty yuan in cash, a gold watch, and a gold ring. After the robbery, the bandits fled towards Shanwan. Afterwards, Weng and others reported the incident to the Fourth Public Security Bureau and requested an investigation. Director Fan of the bureau immediately ordered Patrol Chief Wang Zhenbin of the precinct to pursue the stolen goods. Around six o'clock in the evening yesterday (the 25th), Patrol Chief Wang led five or six police officers in disguise to ambush the scene of the incident. He also ordered another plainclothes police officer to pose as a pedestrian walking on the road. Sure enough, four bandits suddenly emerged from Songfen, intending to rob. The police officer, upon seeing this, sounded a police whistle. The ambushing police officers, upon hearing the signal, stepped forward to arrest them. One bandit was caught on the spot, and the original stolen goods were found on his person. The other three escaped. Patrol Chief Wang then took the captured bandit to the bureau, where Director Fan conducted a preliminary interrogation. The bandit confessed his name as Sun Zhongying, a native of Suzhou, twenty-seven years old, and a soldier in the Fourth Company of the Second Battalion of the 522nd Regiment of the 211th Brigade of the 87th Division in Nanjing. He confessed that he had deserted from Wuxi three days ago and had resorted to robbery. After obtaining the confession, Director Fan immediately prepared a document and submitted it to the General Bureau for interrogation. At the same time, Patrol Chief Wang and the First Precinct continued to apprehend one suspect each, and investigations are currently underway.

Overturned Pig Boat in Changzhou, Lives Lost 108

In Liuqiao, District 18 of Wuyi, the son of a farmer named Liu Laosan, along with villagers, loaded several piglets onto a small boat to sell at Longhutang. On the evening before last, while returning with the empty boat, they encountered a sudden gust of wind and were accidentally hit by a large boat, causing the three people on board to lose their balance and fall into the river. Despite attempts to rescue them, Liu Laosan's son could not be found. On the morning of the 25th, his body was discovered near Xiaoxin Bridge, and his family went to identify it.

Zhenjiang Civil Affairs Department Appoints County Patrol Officers 109

Gu Renfa, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, yesterday appointed Lü Qingyun and Cai Ruquan as patrol officers of the Second and Third Groups of the First Squadron of the Chongming County Water Patrol Team; Shen Jizhou as the Director of the Third Public Security Bureau of Shanghai County; Chen Hanbo as the Director of the Fourth Public Security Bureau of Liyang County; and Lü Baochen, Jiao Jitung, and Tang Xinheng as patrol officers of the Third, Fourth, and Fifth Public Security Bureaus of Changshu County. The appointment orders have been issued separately.

Notorious Bandit Gu Henglou Arrested in Yangzhou 110

The Jiangdu Detective Team previously cracked a kidnapping case in the Jurong area, arrested the bandits, and rescued the victims. According to the confessions of the bandits, many accomplices were involved. They subsequently arrested more bandits in Zhenjiang and the eastern townships of the county, and seized firearms, boats, and stolen goods. From the confession of the arrested bandit Zhou Er, it was learned that Gu Henglou, who lives near Xinghua Bridge outside the North Gate of Taixian County, has many followers, mostly bandits. Gu sits and distributes the spoils, and Wang Xiaobianzi is Gu's only henchman, committing numerous crimes. After obtaining the confession, County Magistrate Ma secretly ordered Police Captain Zhu Xinke and Detective Li to disguise themselves and go to Tai to investigate. They learned that Gu has considerable influence in Taixian County, lives in a large Western-style house, behaves extravagantly, and associates with officials and gentry. Local people mostly call him "Second Master Gu." The team leader and others initially did not dare to act rashly, so they first submitted a document to the Taixian County Government, requesting assistance from the team. Detectives first entered the door, pretending to be Gu's followers, and were admitted. Before they could speak a few words, the detectives drew their guns, preventing any outcry. They then notified the detectives outside the door to enter and search the house. They found a box cannon and a pistol, as well as more than thirty packets of red pills. At the same time, they arrested Wang Xiaobianzi in the Xiaba area. They dispatched a special ship to escort them to Yangzhou. It is said that Gu is fifty-one years old, very strong, and has been in Tai for many years, possessing considerable assets. Wang is thirty years old. Both are from Funing. It is said that in 1930, the Hua Fei murder case in Ganshu Town, District 8 of the county, where Hua Fei held a birthday celebration for his mother, was committed by them. Wang was involved in the "First Army Under Heaven" discovered at Luyang Lake recently, serving as the captain, with most of the weapons and ammunition being provided by Gu. Many other major robbery cases are also involved.

Fierce Battle Between Civilians and Bandits in Dongjiadun, Gaoyou 111

District 10 of this county was occupied by a large group of bandits for several months this summer. Later, the county government telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Chen, who sent Battalion Commander Li Jiuzeng to lead a team to suppress the bandits, and the bandits fled elsewhere. When Battalion Commander Li was transferred away, the bandits sneaked back to Gaoyou. At six o'clock in the morning the day before yesterday, about eighty bandits suddenly appeared in Dongjiadun, District 10, each carrying firearms, planning to occupy the area. The township head sent someone to sound the gong, gathering more than two hundred members of the civil defense, who opened fire on the bandits. Until eight o'clock the next morning, the bandit forces were unable to withstand and fled to the southeast. In this battle, the bandit side suffered more than ten casualties, and four male and female bandits were arrested. On the civil defense side, one township head and twelve members were killed in action.

Verdict Announced in Nantong Fratricide and Dismemberment Case 112

In Tongyi, in the Houyouzha area, a madman named Wu Xiaodaoshi killed his elder brother Wu Changfu in a tragic case of dismemberment and skinning. The murderer was taken to the court by neighbors. After forensic examination by the criminal court, it was determined that the murderer was suffering from intermittent mental illness. The verdict was announced on the 25th, sentencing him to twelve years of imprisonment with commutation.

Search and Arrest Fugitive Bandits in Four Townships 113

The Nantong County Government, with the winter defense approaching, decided to first search and arrest fugitive bandits in the four townships. It was decided to hold a joint meeting of the Defense Committee and district chiefs on November 4th to conduct a household registration investigation and sign joint guarantee agreements. In addition, the Seventh District Commissioner's Office will transfer a suppression team to search in separate routes to clear the source of bandits.

Song Ziwen Actively Prepares Finances, Consults with Zou Lin and Others Yesterday Morning, Seeking Ways to Fund Red Army Suppression, Rumors of Passivity are False 114

Finance Minister Song Ziwen summoned Vice Minister of Finance Zou Lin and other senior officials to the Ministry of Finance office at around eleven o'clock yesterday morning to discuss important financial matters, which lasted for a long time. It is reported that Mr. Song has been actively raising funds for finance in recent days. Although the issue of funding the Red Army suppression is more difficult, Mr. Song has repeatedly stated that he is also planning for it. Therefore, rumors of passive resignation, etc., are not true. According to relevant sources, the difficulty of the central government's finances is an undeniable fact. Those in power at this time should embrace the spirit of shared hardship, work hard, and strive for a way out in the thorny journey. There is no such thing as passivity or activity. If someone else takes over, no one would be unwilling to unload their responsibilities early.

Finance Minister Song Streamlines National Salt Tax, Revenue Has Shown Improvement in the Past Two Months, Approximately Eight Million Yuan Per Month 115

Since returning from Europe, Finance Minister Song Ziwen has greatly streamlined the national salt tax. It is reported that in the past two months, revenue has shown improvement, approximately eight million yuan per month. It is understood that Mr. Song is now revising the salt tax rates in various regions, slightly increasing the rates in areas with lighter salt tax and slightly reducing the rates in areas with heavier salt tax, striving to gradually balance the national salt tax. At the same time, he is trying to facilitate transportation as much as possible, so that future salt tax revenue can gradually increase.

Newly Appointed Envoy to Mexico Huang Yunsu Will Soon Set Sail, Departing Tomorrow Morning at Three O'Clock on the McKinley 116

Newly appointed Envoy to Mexico Huang Yunsu, after receiving his appointment, immediately prepared to go to Mexico to take office. He visited important figures in Nanjing and Lushan, including Wang and Jiang, to request diplomatic instructions. He is scheduled to set sail on the President McKinley at three o'clock tomorrow morning (the 28th). Envoy Huang Yunsu is from Taishan County, Guangdong Province. He studied in the United States in his youth. Because he hated the corrupt politics of the Manchu Qing Dynasty, he and his comrades, including Li Shinan, founded the Young China Society to conduct innovative research on domestic politics. The Young China Society was later reorganized into the American Tongmenghui, and Envoy Huang joined at that time, founding the Chinese Youth Morning Post to promote revolution and awaken the patriotism of overseas Chinese in the Americas. Later, when Premier Sun arrived in the United States, he and Premier Sun went to various ports to raise funds to assist the revolution. He contributed greatly to the Wuchang Uprising in 1911. After that, he returned to China with Premier Sun. With the establishment of the Provisional Government of Nanjing, he was appointed as the Guangdong Envoy of Comfort. When the government moved north, Envoy Huang, being young, was unwilling to enter the official career prematurely. The Labor Bureau deeply appreciated his ambition and sent him to study in the United States, where he entered George Washington and Columbia Universities, devoting himself to the study of political economy, earning master's and bachelor's degrees. After returning to China, he successively served as secretary of the Grand Marshal's Office, member of the Guangdong Education Committee, member of the General Headquarters Ordnance Committee, director of the Guangzhou Finance Bureau. After the cooperation between Ning and Han, he served as a counselor of the National Government, secretary of the National Government, and standing committee member of the Financial Design Committee of the Ministry of Finance. He was then appointed as Consul to Honolulu, and transferred to Consul General in San Francisco. After several years, he was ordered to return to China, traveling to Europe and the United States to investigate the situation of diplomacy, politics, and economy. Envoy Huang is very familiar with American diplomacy and the situation of overseas Chinese. He is very happy to be appointed to Mexico this time. It is reported that Envoy Huang is particularly concerned about the current situation of overseas Chinese in Mexico and will follow the government's instructions and solicit opinions from all parties to work hard for the friendship between China and Mexico and to seek happiness for the overseas Chinese.

Wanxian Suddenly Reports Bandit Alarms, Sichuan Guild Stops Handling Shanghai Goods, Foreign Ships Still Operate, but Freight Rates Slightly Increase 117

This time, the Red Bandits disturbed Sichuan, first clashing with Liu Cunhou's troops near Xuanhan in the Qiaowan River, Jiangdu River, and Shuangmiaochang area, and then advanced to Luojiangkou near Suicheng, the situation is tense. Reinforcements from all directions are gathering in Qixia, Kai County, and are scheduled to launch a general offensive against Xuan and Sui on the 28th and 29th of this month. The bandit army invading Xuan and Sui is now advancing from Guang'an Shunning across the Jialing River to attack Wanxian, resulting in a sudden tightening of the situation in Wanxian. People have already begun to flee downstream. Various public organizations in Wanxian have telegraphed Liu Xiang for emergency help and requested troops to defend the city to protect the commercial port.

Sichuan Ships Requisitioned 118

Upon receiving the report, Liu Xiang believed that Wanxian was an important commercial port in the lower reaches of the Sichuan River and a necessary stop for ships on the upper Yangtze River, so it must be fully defended. Therefore, he immediately transferred 7,000 troops from Chongqing to Wanxian by waterway. However, due to the urgency of the military situation, there was no time to delay, so he requisitioned ships on the upper reaches of the Sichuan River specifically for transport. Six Chinese merchant ships on the Chongqing-Yichang line have all been requisitioned to transport troops, so that, except for Minsheng, all other Chinese ships between Yichang, Wanxian, and Chongqing are supplying troop transport.

Goods Halted 119

Most of the goods shipped from Shanghai to Wanxian are textiles, cotton yarn, sugar, and sundry goods. At this time, the river water has not yet sharply receded, and the customer gangs are rushing to ship. However, due to the sudden bandit scare, in order to avoid danger and maintain capital, an urgent telegram was sent to Shanghai, ordering the Sichuan gang merchants in Shanghai to immediately stop handling goods bound for Wanxian. Those that have been handled but not yet loaded should be stopped from shipping as soon as possible. Those that have already been shipped and are en route should be unloaded in Hankou. The Sichuan gang merchants in Shanghai have all complied with the telegram and stopped handling goods.

Foreign Ships Operate 120

A certain gentleman in charge of the Jiejiang Company told reporters yesterday that because Wanxian is tense due to the bandit alarm, there are no more Shanghai goods, and Chinese merchant ships on the Sichuan River are mostly for military use. However, foreign merchant ships can still sail because they have the protection of their respective national warships. Therefore, the upper Yangtze River ships of Jiejiang (American), Taikoo (British), and Nissin (Japanese) can still operate. However, the freight for goods loaded from Shanghai to the upper Yangtze River will increase by about one-tenth. However, this is not because Wanxian is tense and there are no Chinese ships, but because rates are usually slightly higher during the shallow water season. As for the situation in Wanxian, it is indeed extremely tense. The large army transferred from the upper reaches has arrived, or it can be hoped that nothing will happen. However, commercial transportation has been interrupted, and the market will inevitably be affected.

Li Shizeng Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 121

Central Committee Member Li Shizeng arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon. After arriving in Nanjing from Beijing, he took the Beijing-Shanghai express train from the capital at around 8 o'clock yesterday morning and arrived in Shanghai at around 2 o'clock in the afternoon. He then returned to his residence in the French Concession to rest. As for the date of Mr. Li's departure to France to attend the International Cultural Promotion Association, he said that it cannot be predicted yet, but it will not be far off.

Municipal Party Headquarters Telegraphed Yesterday to Comfort the Frontline Soldiers Suppressing Bandits 122

The Municipal Party Headquarters, believing that the Red Bandits are entrenched in the mountains and forests of Jiangxi, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei, resembling roaming bandits, and that the frontline soldiers are making efforts to suppress them with great success, so that complete suppression can be expected, the department telegraphed to the front to express condolences and encouragement. The original text read: "To Chairman Jiang in Nanchang and all frontline soldiers: The Red Bandits have plagued Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei for several years, poisoning the atmosphere, turning houses into ruins, and committing rape, plunder, and murder, which is absolutely inhuman. They dare to take advantage of the national army's resistance against Japan, seizing the opportunity to create chaos and harming the rear, which is a heinous crime, condemned by both humans and gods. However, the Red Bandits are entrenched in the mountains and forests, relying on dangerous terrain, fleeing here and there, resembling roaming bandits. It is difficult to eliminate them after several years of hard work. At this time of Pacific crisis and drastic changes in the international situation, if the bandit scourge is not eliminated and the foundation of the country is stabilized, how can we cope with this extraordinary situation? Fortunately, our Chairman Jiang does not avoid hardship and personally visits the bandit area, making plans and commanding with certainty, winning every battle, saving the compatriots of the four provinces from water and fire, and securing the nation and the people on a solid foundation. We are waiting for the final great success and establishing an unparalleled great cause. We are looking forward to it with admiration and are sending out the party members and the public to work hard and eliminate the communist work in the rear to support the front. We hereby telegraph our condolences and hope you will take note. The Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipality of the Chinese Kuomintang bows and seals."

Negotiation Process for Eight Rice Merchants to Cancel Order of Japanese Rice, Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association Held Emergency Meeting Yesterday 123

According to the Dagong News Agency, the case of eight rice merchants in this city, including Shenfeng, ordering 25,000 bags of old rice from Japan has been met with serious opposition from all sectors. The Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association sent personnel to investigate the truth and strictly ordered the merchants to cancel the contract quickly. The managers of the eight rice merchants then negotiated the cancellation procedures. At 4 p.m. the day before yesterday, a settlement was reached, with a compensation of 10,000 yuan for losses. The signed order was mutually returned and invalidated. The Miscellaneous Grain Association held an emergency meeting yesterday to report on the process and announce it to the industry. The details are recorded as follows:

Cancellation Process 124

The eight rice merchants, including Shenfeng, received warnings from the Miscellaneous Grain, Oil Cake, and Industry Association, and were strictly ordered to cancel the contract with the foreign firm that purchased the rice as soon as possible. The managers of each firm met at Shenfeng Shop in Doushi Street at 1 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 24th) to discuss the procedures. It was initially said that Gu Xinyi of Yongda had not returned to Shanghai from attending a meeting in Jiangxi, and it was proposed to postpone the matter. However, more than half of the firms of the eight merchants rapidly proceeded with the matter in order to avoid unexpected events. They immediately appointed Wang Yintang, manager of Shenfeng Shop, Chen Ziyi, manager of Changfeng Shop, and Zhou Yuting, manager of Dafeng Shop, as plenipotentiary representatives to negotiate the cancellation with the American firm Handolai.

Cancellation Negotiation 125

The three appointed managers immediately prepared a letter on the same day (the 24th) at 3 p.m. and went to the American firm Handolai at 29 Sichuan Road to negotiate with Lin Bozao, the person in charge of the firm, but no result was achieved. After the representatives returned to their firms, they discussed the second step. On the next day (the 25th), they continued to negotiate with Lin Bozao. The foreign firm proposed to compensate one yuan per bag of the rice for the loss, totaling 24,866 yuan, before the order could be invalidated. The two sides negotiated for a long time. Until 4 p.m., the final result was that 10,000 yuan was determined as compensation. On the spot, the signed purchase orders were mutually returned and invalidated.

10,000 Yuan Compensation 126

Yesterday morning, the American firm Handolai sent a letter to Gu Xinyi, manager of Yongda Shop, stating, "Dear Sir, We have received several bank drafts from your firm dated November 5, totaling 10,000 yuan. This payment is the compensation for the cancellation of 24,866 bags of Rangoon small broken white rice completed on the 9th of this month. The order is attached herewith for cancellation. Please also return the order issued by our firm as soon as possible. Sincerely, M. Heidlen, Yongda, Rencheng, Changyi, Dingtaide, Dafeng, Shenfeng, Changmao, Wanxingyu."

Order Invalidated 127

The full text of the order mutually signed by the eight rice merchants, including Shenfeng, and the American firm Handolai on the 9th of this month is in English. The translation is as follows: "The terms and conditions of the sale and purchase agreed upon by our firm (Handolai) and your firm (i.e., the eight merchants including Shenfeng) are as follows: Quality: All white rice, for small factories, old rice. Quantity: 25 pounds, 25,000 bags, with a tolerance of 5%. Shipping date: Within this month, to be shipped from Chinese or foreign warehouses. Price: 6.30 yuan per 200 pounds. Note: Other matters shall be handled in accordance with customs regulations." The said order has been mutually exchanged and invalidated.

Reply to the Association 128

The eight rice merchants, including Shenfeng, jointly replied to the Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association after the cancellation, stating, "Respectfully replying, We received your letter on October 23, instructing us to work together to cancel the 24,866 bags of small broken rice ordered this time with the foreign firm as soon as possible, otherwise the rice will be sold by the association in accordance with the previous resolution, the surplus will be used for charitable purposes, and the loss will be borne by us, etc. Previously, we received a similar warning from the Bean and Rice Industry Association. We have been negotiating with the foreign firm several times and have achieved results. We respectfully report the origin of this matter for your examination. The rice ordered by our firms from the American firm Handolai is small broken rice from Rangoon. As for where it comes from and on which ship it is loaded, it is the business of the foreign firm, and we have no way of knowing. If we knew that it was shipped from Shanghai by a Japanese ship, we would not dare to do this even if we were foolish. Moreover, privately importing Japanese goods is a kind of secret deal under the current circumstances. Even if we want to take this risk, we are afraid of not being careful enough to keep it secret. How can there be a reason to publicly allocate the rice to eight firms and accept the rice willingly? Just by this counter-evidence, the original intention of our firms to order foreign rice this time can be more than half understood. Only because Handolai was initially selling the rice, our firms believed that the dumping of this batch of goods in Shanghai would affect the market price when the new grain was coming into the market. Therefore, we agreed to purchase it equally to maintain the current rice price so that it would not be suppressed by the dumping of this foreign rice, which would harm the economy of farmers. We did not expect that this batch of foreign rice, according to the investigation of your investigators, was actually shipped from Shanghai by a Japanese ship. This is really unexpected by our firms and deeply regrettable. Before receiving your letter, we immediately canceled the contract with the foreign firm, and the loss fee of 10,000 yuan was agreed upon in the negotiations on the afternoon of October 25. We paid the money and signed the contract this morning, completely canceling the contract. All the orders have been mutually exchanged and invalidated. Our firms know that the rice is sold by your association, even if there is a loss, it will not be as much as 10,000 yuan, and we must voluntarily negotiate the cancellation to bear this huge loss, which is precisely to show the sincerity of our firms. The cancellation documents will be submitted for verification when your association holds a meeting. Special reply to the Shanghai Miscellaneous Grain, Oil Cake, and Industry Association, Yongda, Shenfeng, Rencheng, Changyi, Dingtaide, Dafeng, Changmao, Wanxingyu, etc."

Meeting of Miscellaneous Grain Industry 129

Yesterday afternoon at 3 p.m., the Miscellaneous Grain, Oil Cake, and Industry Association convened an emergency meeting on the third floor of the Miscellaneous Grain Exchange on Minguo Road. Chairman Chen Yuming reported on the cancellation of the contract by the eight merchants, and the important resolutions on prohibiting the purchase of foreign rice were decided on the spot. The details are recorded as follows:

Attending Committee Members 130

More than ten people attended, including Fang Yusheng, Chen Yuming, He Xianggudi, Guan Renshan, Xie Yanglin, He Quansheng, Cao Xingeng, Zhu Xiangsheng, Shang Zuocheng, Jiang Zisheng, Zhu Zixiang, Yu Bingwen, and others. More than 200 members of the industry were present. The atmosphere at the meeting was very tense. The meeting was officially announced to be open at 3 p.m., and Chen Yuming was elected as the temporary chairman, and Kong Shulin as the secretary.

Resolutions 131

First, Chairman Chen Yuming presented the eight merchants' explanation about the cancellation of their contracts, and the report was approved with letter. Afterwards, the discussions started on: (1)According to the eight companies including Shenfeng's response (Letter seen earlier) This time, the rice that was ordered has already completed contract cancellation, please look into the matter (Resolution) The rice ordered by the eight companies including Shenfeng was handled and negotiated towards Handolai trading company. Paying a loss of 10,000 yuan, and retrieving the completed paperwork, as of this morning (yesterday morning) all contracts are fully cancelled. This loss is one's own doing, a warning for future actions. All documents and receipts will be stored inside of the association, a notice will be given to those of the same trade, for those who dare to go against this rule, secretly completing orders, once found, they will be expelled from the Association and considered a public enemy. (2)In recent years the production of local crops were large and bountiful, and the prices have fallen. The economical state of farming villages are on the verge of ruins. The association suggests that people in the trade do not complete orders for foreign rice. The association will work together to upkeep the economical state of the trade (Resolution) Passed.

Public Notice to Fellow Traders 132

After the meeting, a temporary announcement was issued, stating that it was a notice regarding the matter of Shen Feng and eight other firms ordering foreign rice. Our association has convened several emergency meetings to discuss and decided to strictly order the eight fellow traders to terminate the contract with the foreign firm for the foreign rice. Now, we have received a reply from the said fellow traders (see the previous reply). Based on this, another emergency meeting was convened on the 16th of this month (the resolution is omitted above), and these matters have been recorded. It is appropriate to record and announce this matter, and we respectfully hope that all fellow traders in the trade will take note. This is a special announcement. October 26th, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

Hebei Finance Director Visited Finance Minister Song Yesterday Morning to Report the Province's Financial Difficulties and Request Mr. Song's Approval for Relief of the Contribution Payment 133

Lu Muting, the Director of Finance of Hebei Province, under the order of Yu Xuezhong, the Chairman of the province, arrived in Shanghai from Peiping by train the day before yesterday to pay his respects to Finance Minister Song Ziwen, to report on the financial difficulties of the province and request approval for relief of the contribution payment. Mr. Lu went to Mr. Song's residence on Qiqi Road at 10:30 yesterday morning to pay his respects. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency specially visited Mr. Lu at his lodging in the afternoon, but Mr. Lu was out. Secretary Zhang Mujiang met with the reporter instead. According to him, the financial difficulties of Hebei were very detailed. The details are as follows:

Reduced Revenue 134

Mr. Zhang first stated that Hebei's revenue decreased by more than ten million last year due to the abolition of the Likin tax. Later, when the war broke out, tax revenue in the war zone completely stopped. Although the war has now ended, twelve counties under the jurisdiction of Hebei Province have not fully recovered to their original state, and they have also been ordered to appropriately exempt land taxes in the war zone, resulting in a sharp decrease in revenue of more than one million. In addition, the areas affected by the Yellow River floods will have to reduce revenue by more than ten thousand, he said.

Increased Expenditure 135

As for expenditures, the monthly salary for the security forces alone requires 150,000, and the monthly salary for incorporating the troops of Li Jichun and others requires another 50,000 to 60,000. Including other expenses, the total monthly increase compared to before is more than 300,000.

Budget Deficit 136

According to the budget, the annual income is only over 19 million, while the annual expenditure is over 27 million. Now that income has decreased and expenditure has increased, and the annual increase in security force salaries is more than 3 million, the annual expenditure cannot be less than 30 million. Therefore, the deficit is more than ten million, he said.

Contribution Relief 137

The stipulated contribution to the central government is originally over 800,000 per month, but it has not been fully paid. The previous payment to the North China Financial Reorganization Committee was only 600,000 to 700,000, and after the abolition of the Likin tax, it was only 500,000 to 600,000. Now, all military expenses in North China are actually borne by Hebei. Now, the central government has ordered the Finance Department to allocate the contribution to the Finance Department of the Political Affairs Reorganization Committee on schedule, otherwise, they will be punished, or deducted from the military expenses. Therefore, under the order of Chairman Yu, he came to Shanghai to pay his respects to Finance Minister Song to report the actual difficulties and request approval for relief. After meeting with Finance Minister Song, he will return to the north tomorrow to report, he said.

Specializes in handling personal matters and will return to the North in a few days. Shanghai Times News Agency reported from this city that Wang Kemin, a member of the Peiping Political Affairs Committee, has reportedly resigned from his position as Director of the Finance Department after the Political Affairs Committee decided to reorganize. On the 19th, he was ordered to take various documents, such as the reorganization plan of the Political Affairs Committee, to Nanjing from Peiping, where he consulted with President Wang and others. Now, Mr. Wang arrived in Shanghai by train at 8:00 yesterday morning. He is here to handle personal matters and will return to the North in a few days, it is said.

Central Government Sends Li Renzhu to Shanghai to Investigate the Truth of the Electric Power Strike Fei Xindun and Du Yuesheng Negotiate Mediation The General Labor Union Issued a Call for Assistance Announcement Yesterday on Behalf of the Workers 143

Dagong News Agency reported that since the Shanghai Electric Power Company strike broke out, the Municipal General Labor Union, considering the matter to be of great importance, telegraphed the Central Party Department's People's Movement Committee, requesting them to send personnel to Shanghai to jointly discuss and handle the matter with the Party and government as soon as possible. Now, the central government has sent Li Renzhu, the Director-General of the People's Movement Committee, to Shanghai yesterday to investigate the truth. The Municipal Council is negotiating solutions. The Municipal General Labor Union yesterday re-issued a call for assistance announcement for the power workers (see the advertisement column). The details are recorded separately as follows:

Central Government Sends Personnel to Shanghai 144

The Central People's Movement Committee, considering the Shanghai Electric Power strike to be a serious situation, previously telegraphed the local Party and government authorities, requesting them to mediate as soon as possible. Since the strike has not yet been resolved, the committee specially sent its Director-General, Li Renzhu, to Shanghai yesterday to investigate the truth in order to find a way to handle it. After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Li went to the Municipal Party Department yesterday morning to meet with Tong Xingbai, a member of the Standing Committee, and Zhou Funong, the Director of the People's Movement Section. He inquired in detail about the cause and process of the strike. Later, the Municipal Party Department sent a cadre, Long Peiyun, to meet with Zhu Xuefan and Shao Xubai, members of the General Labor Union, at 3:00 PM yesterday. The two of them presented a detailed account of the handling process of the case, the current situation, the proof documents guaranteeing workers previously established by the Municipal Council, and the company's violation of promises and unwarranted dismissal of Chinese workers. They also summoned Xu Hongsheng, a representative of the Fourth District Water and Electricity Labor Union, to ask questions about the truth of the dispute in great detail. It is heard that Mr. Li still has important matters in Nanjing, so he returned to Nanjing last night to report to the central government first. He will still need to come to Shanghai tonight to continue the investigation. In addition, Bao Huaguo, the Fourth Section Chief of the Labor Department specially sent by the Ministry of Industry to Shanghai for investigation, has completed his work and took the Shanghai-Nanjing train yesterday afternoon to report back.

Fei and Du Negotiate Solutions 145

Since the electric power strike broke out, various organizations in this city, considering the matter to be related to the safety of the entire society, have sent letters to the board of directors of the Municipal Council, requesting them to mediate as soon as possible. After receiving the letters, the Municipal Council sent the Western Director-General Pei'er to negotiate with the company's Taipan, Huo Pogensi, and sent letters to summon representatives of the four electric power workers to inquire about their attitudes in order to find a way to mediate. At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Director-General Fei Xindun invited Municipal Councilor Du Yuesheng to the bureau to negotiate solutions and decided to proceed with mediation immediately. In addition, Chinese Directors Yu Qiaqing and Yuan Ludeng also consulted with Director-General Pei'er on everything. Therefore, the Municipal Council has been quite active in handling the strike in fact. However, whether a solution can be obtained immediately depends on the sincerity and concessions of both parties.

Current Situation Inside the Two Factories 146

In order to understand the current situation inside the two factories since the power workers' strike has been going on for a long time, the Dagong News Agency reporter specially investigated various parties yesterday. It is reported that the new factory (power generation room) has a total of 30 electric furnaces, divided into four rooms. The number one furnace room has eight furnaces, and four are currently burning. The number two furnace room has eight furnaces, and all are currently burning. It is found that the furnaces in this room have not been fully lit since the May 30th incident. This time, they had to be fully lit to maintain the current because of the workers' strike. The number three furnace room has ten furnaces, and seven are currently burning. The remaining three are broken. Because no one is repairing them after the workers' strike, they cannot be used. The number four furnace room has four furnaces, and three are currently burning. One was dismantled before the strike, but it has not been repaired yet. Moreover, the furnaces are gradually damaged because they are burned every day without being repaired. The workshop has a total of fourteen generators. Generators number eight and nine could previously generate 20,000 watts each. Now, due to a lack of maintenance, the power generation has decreased to less than 10,000 watts. The other three coal hoisting cars are also slightly damaged. All projects for installing antennas and laying underground cables in the old factory are currently suspended. Although the company has hired more than 30 White Russians, it is of no avail.

Statement from the Go-Slow Committee 147

According to a statement issued by the Electric Power Company Employees' Go-Slow Committee, after the sudden assassination of employee Chen Qinglu, many outsiders suspect that it is related to the strike. In fact, Chen Qinglu was very sympathetic to the strike. When the Lianyi Society held a social conference at the Youth Propaganda Group on the 11th, Chen was elected as one of the go-slow committee members. Later, due to the limited number of places, Chen narrowly missed being elected. He then joined the picket team as a secret investigator and worked very hard. He was eventually forced to resume work due to pressure from his family (his sister had repeatedly gone to the society to argue with Chen). Now, the company's declaration that the victimized employee had repeatedly refused to join the strike before the incident is based on what? As for the fact that loyal and diligent employees were repeatedly subjected to violent pressure before the strike incident to force them to pay part of their wages for the strike, it is even more unfounded. In short, the company, in its imperial capitalist face, does not hesitate to use its despicable means and apply poisonous schemes to destroy the labor movement. This kind of trick only shows that its efforts are in vain.

After Dye Industry Workers Stopped Dyeing, Labor and Capital Negotiated Yesterday with No Results 151

The dispute between the labor side demanding the restoration of the old contract and the separation of liquor money in the silk, satin, and cotton cloth dyeing industry in this city has not yet been resolved after the suspension of dyeing passenger and freight goods. All parties are paying close attention to it. The capital side's fellow traders have organized a Business Reorganization Committee to deal with the go-slow incident. Yesterday, a joint meeting of labor and capital representatives was convened. Representatives of the labor side's silk and cotton cloth office, Tan Xirong, Wang Zishan, and Jin Aosheng, representatives of silk and satin, Shen Shuangxi, Wang Guoxiang, and Han Baoxian, and representatives of the capital side, Pan Jiaming, Fan Ruihua, and Sheng Xingqing, etc. attended. First, Pan Jiaming, a representative of the capital side, spoke, saying that your labor union's demand for the restoration of the liquor money in the old contract and the go-slow incident have occurred. If we persist in this for a long time and cannot resolve it, not only will our industry suffer a direct and great loss, but it will also have a great impact on the silk weaving industry. The silk weaving industry has been in a slump in recent years, reaching its peak. Moreover, at this time when the autumn season is the time to sell off accumulated debts, the dyeing industry's go-slow, the goods cannot be dyed, and the sales will be suddenly hit hard. The indirect losses in the meantime are even more unbearable than those of our industry. Now, the overall opinion of the capital side is to accommodate the guarantee of the restoration of the liquor money in your labor union, and one side will resume work immediately to reduce the losses of all parties. Tan Borong, a representative of the labor side, spoke, saying that our labor union's demand to restore the old contract treatment and separate the liquor money is the unanimous movement of all workers. We will not resume work for a day until we achieve our goal. Our determination is very firm, and there is no room for compromise. We hope that your side will sincerely accept and seek a one-time solution. As a result, the two sides could not get close. After the meeting, a representative of the capital side told visitors that he (self-proclaimed) did not want to participate in this unfortunate labor-capital dispute in our industry. However, he was forced by the public opinion of his fellow traders and could not refuse, so he reluctantly took on the task, hoping to seek a compromise between labor and capital on the principle of mutual benefit. Unexpectedly, the situation cannot be resolved in a short time. He plans to go to Peiping in a few days to avoid everything, etc. At the same time, the capital side's Business Reorganization Committee held its third representative meeting to discuss important cases to be dealt with.

Shallow Water in Baihe River Blocks Ships Xin Ming Aground for Three Hours Before Getting Out of the Shallows 153

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Ming ship left Tianjin's Zizhu Forest this time, passed through Tanggu, and returned to Shanghai. In the Baihe River, it encountered low tide, causing it to run aground. It was found that the ship's draft was 11 feet 5 inches after loading, and the Baihe River's tide was only 10 feet, causing it to be blocked and run aground. However, the ship could get out of the shallows as soon as the tide rose, and there was no damage to the hull. The bureau received a telegram from the shipowner yesterday, stating that the ship could arrive in Shanghai this afternoon, only slightly delayed by a few hours of the journey. In addition, the Guangji ship of the Wenzhou route of the bureau encountered a strong wind on the way, but fortunately the shipowner took precautions in advance to avoid it, so the arrival in Wenzhou was slightly later than the original scheduled time.

Customs Notice Measures for Recovering Tax Payments and Giving Awards Informants Can Get 40% of the Penalty 154

Customs Tax Affairs Division Bolesdorf has issued a notice on measures for awarding awards for recovering tax payments based on informant reports. The notice was posted yesterday, saying, "This is to notify that the Customs' measures for awarding awards for recovering tax payments based on informant reports are listed on the left, and everyone should know them. This is a special notice. (1) If a merchant's previously underpaid tax payments are recovered due to an informant report, and a penalty is imposed, 20% of the tax payments recovered within the previous three years or 40% of the penalty imposed will be awarded, whichever is greater. However, this award, if given according to the tax payments recovered within the previous three years, is limited to 100,000 national currency. (2) If a merchant's previously underpaid tax payments are recovered due to an informant report, but no penalty is imposed, 20% of the tax payments recovered within the previous three years will be awarded, also limited to 100,000 national currency."

Pudong Electric Company Lays Underwater Cable Across the River; Public Works and Public Safety Bureaus Issue Notices to Ships Regarding Construction from Wuquan Road, North Bund to Taojia Mao, East Pudong 156

Pudong Electric Company, with the order of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, contacted Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to receive electricity. The two companies signed an electricity supply contract in February of this year and agreed to first lay an underwater cable from the north of Wuquan Road, north of Jungong Road, east of the Bund in Zhabei, across the Huangpu River to Taojiazhai in the Gaohang District of Pudong. The cable has already been ordered from England and transported to Shanghai. They have already begun setting up signs marking the cable crossing to prevent ships from damaging it by dropping anchor. These signs will be installed before the cable is laid to warn passing ships.

After receiving notice from the Pudong Electric Company regarding the installation of the underwater cable across the river, the Municipal Public Works and Public Safety Bureaus jointly issued a notice, stating: "Notice is hereby given that the Pudong Electric Company has submitted a report stating that the company signed an electricity supply contract with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company in February of this year, agreeing to first lay an underwater cable from the Bund north of Wuquan Road, north of Jungong Road, east of the Bund in Zhabei (approximately 1,130 meters south of the Qiujiang River Port), across the Huangpu River to the Pudong Electric Company's substation in Taojiazhai, Gaohang District, Pudong. The cable has already arrived from England, and construction is planned to begin in mid-October of this year. Warning signs in Chinese, 'Cable Crossing, No Anchoring,' and in English, 'Cable Arosing,' are being installed on both banks before the underground cables are laid and should be completed quickly. Fearing that ships traveling in the river will arbitrarily drop anchor in that area, damaging the cable and hindering the flow of electricity, a special report has been submitted requesting inspection, joint issuance of a notice, and strict prohibition of all ships from anchoring in that area. Otherwise, if the cable is damaged and power is cut off, the ship responsible will be held liable for all losses suffered by the company and will be severely punished to maintain public utilities, etc. An investigation reveals that if ships are allowed to drop anchor at will where this underwater cable is laid, the cable could easily be damaged. Therefore, it should be strictly prohibited to avoid causing malfunctions. All ships traveling in the Huangpu River must pay attention and must not anchor in that area. Violators will be severely punished without leniency once discovered. Let everyone be warned. This notice is issued by Wen Hong'en, Director of the Public Safety Bureau, and Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Works Bureau."
